# Quest Hub Expansion — Emberwild_DepthPack_GIGA_Part3_2025-12-24_QuestHub_Expansion

1500 grounded quests (QST-3500 → QST-4999).

## QST-3500 — A Map That Lies (Saltmarrow)
- **Giver:** Mire Warden
- **Type:** Collect
- **Objectives:**
  1. Collect **Warden's Ring** (ID 45396).
  2. Collect **Sun-bleached Vest** (ID 47340) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Deliver **Tide-taken Root** (ID 47906) to a local contact.
- **Rewards:**
  - **Moon-stitched Helm** (ID 48346) *or* **Hollowroot Boots** (ID 45686)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.

- **Type:** Sabotage
- **Objectives:**
  1. Collect **Briarbound Pod** (ID 48311).
  2. Collect **Gutterborn Helm** (ID 47163) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Deliver **Lantern-lit Token** (ID 48852) to a local contact.
- **Rewards:**
  - **Harbor-wet Charm** (ID 48912) *or* **Harbor-wet Token** (ID 46861)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.

- **Type:** Sabotage
- **Objectives:**
  1. Collect **Storm-bit Nail** (ID 48273).
  2. Collect **Frostbriar Petal** (ID 46481) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Deliver **Sun-bleached Tally** (ID 45227) to a local contact.
- **Rewards:**
  - **Warden's Lichen** (ID 49444) *or* **Greatwood Seed** (ID 45544)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.
